name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Room (2 bedsÔºâ
info:Stayed in April 2024

info:3 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 28, 2024
msg:This time, I traveled to Xiamen with my parents and children and stayed at Langham Hotel. Overall, I was very satisfied.
Before checking in, the butler Pearl took the initiative to call and ask what other requirements there were for checking in and what time the hotel was. She and her colleague Mila helped coordinate adjacent rooms because they needed to be next to my parents so that they could take care of each other.
The receptionist at the door took the initiative to open the door of the car and take the luggage. They were all quite enthusiastic. The room is quite large, and the bathroom and toilet area is also quite large. There is a large floor-to-ceiling window and a sofa. If you are not too tall and want to sleep alone, you can sleep on this sofa. The double beds can be spliced. What I like most is the bed guard. For a child who is not honest when sleeping, I can finally sleep more peacefully.
There is a thoughtful welcome handwritten by the butler Pearl. The drinks and chips in the small refrigerator are free to eat, and they are replenished once a day for free.
Because each room has two breakfasts, my eldest child, who is 14 years old and over 1.4 meters tall, asked the butler and said that the morning buffet breakfast can be discounted at 80 yuan. This price is acceptable. In the end, because there are many snack bars next to the hotel, one adult did not go to the buffet, so the money was saved.
The cleaning lady was also considerate. She wrote a paragraph by hand, saying that she saw medicine on our table and gave us several more bottles of water.
Let me talk about some minor flaws that I think are common. In fact, this should be a common problem, including the Westin Wanning where I stayed before, as well as five-star hotels in Nanjing, hotels in Sanya, etc., that is, the cleaning problem. After all, it is manually cleaned, and there must be omissions. The reason why I brought it up is that I still hope that the cleaning work can be done better during non-peak periods. Just like smiley faces, caring cards, food, etc., these soft services are liked by customers, but I think if a hotel has good cleaning work, I will like it more even if there are no soft services.
The day before, the child ate potato chips in the room and got them on the carpet. The next day, the aunt did not clean it up. There were potato chips that were not cleaned up in the space between the sofa and the bed. Later, I picked them up and threw them away. There was dust inside the two small towel racks in the bathroom. It must have been there for a long time. I wiped off the light layer, but the dark layer could not be wiped off. On the first day of my stay, I wiped the toilet with a wet wipe. I found a circle of black stains around the circular joint where the toilet lid was lifted up. I wiped it off with a tissue. Overall, Langham is still very good, with some minor flaws. I hope it can be improved. I prefer this hotel when I come to Xiamen in the future.
----------------------------------------

msg:On my first night in Xiamen, I stayed at the British-style Langham Place in Xiamen. Before I even arrived at the hotel, I called the hotel in advance to ask when I would arrive and if I had any needs for the room layout. I was very impressed even before I checked in.

It was already 17:30 when I arrived at the hotel. It was a rainy day and the traffic jam made me a little motion sick. The guy who checked me in was kind enough to upgrade me to a suite for free and gave me a motion sickness sticker. The beautiful housekeeper Ella also helped me carry my bag and luggage all the way to the room. , the service is really 100 points.

Langham and Langham are both British-style hotels. Beautiful pink elements can be seen everywhere in the hotel lobby, such as pink roses, pink taxis, and pink bears. No girl can resist the temptation of pink. The hall is full of artistic elements, and the art installations everywhere make you feel like you are in a museum. Although it was only the end of November when I checked in, the Chris**as a**osphere in the hotel was already very strong. The huge Chris**as tree was beautifully decorated. I couldn't help but look at it every time I passed by the lobby.

As a business hotel, Langham Place does not have the same charming sea view as Xiamen Sea View Hotel, but you can take a taxi to Guanyin Mountain for 2.5 kilometers. There are not only cafes with great sea views, but also the best place to watch the sunrise in Xiamen, whether for business or tourism. In fact, the location is quite convenient. Next to it is Wanda, where you can eat, drink and have fun.

Although the room is not very luxurious, it is very clean, there are fresh green plants on the coffee table, and the decoration is very warm. The main European suite is very large, more than 80 square meters, with a color TV in the living room and bedroom, making it easy to watch the World Cup in different places at night. The bathtub is quite large and the "Sichuan" toiletries are very useful. The bed is a king-size bed and comes with 8 different types of pillows to choose from, which is good news for people who have trouble sleeping. It's very quiet to sleep at night, and the sound insulation is also very good. When you come back after dinner, the housekeeper Ella will serve you good night sweet soup. The meticulous service is really touching.

Apart from afternoon tea, the most unmissable thing when staying at Langham Place is the Michelin-starred restaurant Mingge. I have eaten at Mingge in Shanghai several times and the taste is outstanding. Business at Xiamen Mingge is also very good at night. The lobby is almost full. The ones are also very delicate and delicious. The bar on the first floor of the hotel has a World Cup co-branded wine package. You can drink and eat while watching the game on the huge screen, which is super cool and has a great a**osphere.

Since I arrived very late on the first day, I didn‚Äôt want to be too tired, so I didn‚Äôt go to the swimming pool and gym to check in. The breakfast snacks on the second day were delicious, overall
